# AI Insights UI Specification

## Overview

This document specifies the user interface design for AI Insights, including chat interface, insight widgets, configuration panels, and integration points throughout the application.

> **Design Philosophy**: "AI should feel like a helpful colleague, not a separate tool."

---

1. [Design Principles](#design-principles)
2. [Chat Interface](#chat-interface)
3. [Quick Insight Panel](#quick-insight-panel)

## Design Principles

### Core Principles

| Principle | Description |
|-----------|-------------|
| **Contextual** | AI appears where users need it, not in a separate app |
| **Non-intrusive** | Suggestions enhance workflow, never interrupt |
| **Transparent** | Always show sources, confidence, and reasoning |
| **Actionable** | Every insight leads to clear next steps |
| **Responsive** | Stream responses, show progress, never block |

### Visual Identity

```typescript
interface AIVisualIdentity {
  // Brand colors
  colors: {
    primary: '#6366f1';           // Indigo - AI brand color
    secondary: '#8b5cf6';         // Purple - accent
    background: {
      light: '#f5f3ff';           // Light purple tint
      dark: '#1e1b4b';            // Dark purple
    };
    confidence: {
      high: '#10b981';            // Green
      medium: '#f59e0b';          // Amber
      low: '#ef4444';             // Red
    };
  };
  
  // Typography
  fonts: {
    assistant: 'Inter';           // Clean, modern
    code: 'JetBrains Mono';       // For code blocks
  };
  
  // Avatar
  avatar: {
    icon: 'sparkles';             // Lucide icon
    shape: 'rounded';             // Rounded square
    animation: 'pulse';           // When thinking
  };
}
```

### Chat Component Specification

```typescript
interface ChatInterfaceProps {
  // Initial context
  context?: {
    shardId?: string;
    shardType?: string;
    scope?: ContextScope;
  };
  
  // Existing conversation
  conversationId?: string;
  
  // Display mode
  mode: 'panel' | 'fullscreen' | 'embedded';
  
  // Size
  width?: number | string;
  height?: number | string;
  
  // Features
  features: {
    streaming: boolean;
    suggestions: boolean;
    feedback: boolean;
    sources: boolean;
    actions: boolean;
    voice: boolean;
    attachments: boolean;
  };
  
  // Callbacks
  onMessageSent?: (message: string) => void;
  onInsightGenerated?: (insight: InsightResponse) => void;
  onActionTriggered?: (action: InsightAction) => void;
  onClose?: () => void;
}
```

### Message Types

```typescript
interface ChatMessage {
  id: string;
  role: 'user' | 'assistant' | 'system';
  content: string;
  timestamp: Date;
  
  // For assistant messages
  metadata?: {
    insightType?: InsightType;
    confidence?: ConfidenceScore;
    citations?: SourceCitation[];
    actions?: InsightAction[];
    charts?: ChartSuggestion[];
    isStreaming?: boolean;
    tokensUsed?: number;
    latencyMs?: number;
  };
  
  // For user messages
  attachments?: Attachment[];
  contextSnapshot?: string[];     // Shard IDs in context
}

interface InsightAction {
  id: string;
  type: 'create_task' | 'schedule_meeting' | 'draft_email' | 'navigate' | 'copy' | 'share';
  label: string;
  icon: string;
  payload: Record<string, any>;
  requiresConfirmation?: boolean;
}
```

### Streaming UI

```typescript
interface StreamingUIState {
  // Typing indicator
  isTyping: boolean;
  typingText: 'Thinking...' | 'Searching...' | 'Analyzing...' | 'Writing...';
  
  // Progressive content
  streamedContent: string;
  cursorPosition: number;
  
  // Progress indicators
  progress?: {
    stage: 'context' | 'generating' | 'grounding' | 'formatting';
    percentage: number;
  };
  
  // Cancel option
  canCancel: boolean;
}
```

### Keyboard Shortcuts

| Shortcut | Action |
|----------|--------|
| `Enter` | Send message |
| `Shift + Enter` | New line |
| `/` | Open template picker |
| `@` | Mention user or shard |
| `â†‘` | Previous message (when input empty) |
| `Cmd/Ctrl + K` | Open command palette |
| `Escape` | Close panel or cancel |

---

## Quick Insight Panel

### Trigger Points

The Quick Insight Panel appears contextually throughout the app:

```

### Quick Actions Configuration

```typescript
interface QuickInsightConfig {
  // Which quick actions to show
  quickActions: QuickAction[];
  
  // Popular questions (generated or predefined)
  popularQuestions: {
    source: 'predefined' | 'generated' | 'learned';
    items: string[];
    maxItems: number;
  };
  
  // Panel behavior
  panel: {
    position: 'right' | 'bottom' | 'modal';
    width: number;
    expandable: boolean;
  };
}

interface QuickAction {
  id: string;
  label: string;
  icon: string;
  insightType: InsightType;
  promptTemplate?: string;
  color?: string;
}

const DEFAULT_QUICK_ACTIONS: QuickAction[] = [
  { id: 'summarize', label: 'Summarize', icon: 'FileText', insightType: 'summary', color: 'blue' },
  { id: 'risks', label: 'Analyze Risks', icon: 'AlertTriangle', insightType: 'analysis', color: 'orange' },
  { id: 'recommend', label: 'Recommend', icon: 'Lightbulb', insightType: 'recommendation', color: 'green' },
  { id: 'compare', label: 'Compare', icon: 'GitCompare', insightType: 'comparison', color: 'purple' },
  { id: 'extract', label: 'Extract Actions', icon: 'ListChecks', insightType: 'extraction', color: 'teal' },
];
```

### Widget Configuration

```typescript
interface InsightWidgetConfig {
  id: string;
  type: 'live_insight' | 'risk_radar' | 'priorities' | 'metrics' | 'activity' | 'custom';
  title: string;
  
  // Insight configuration
  insight: {
    type: InsightType;
    scope: ContextScope;
    template?: string;
    customPrompt?: string;
  };
  
  // Refresh settings
  refresh: {
    auto: boolean;
    intervalMinutes: number;
    onDataChange: boolean;
  };
  
  // Display settings
  display: {
    showConfidence: boolean;
    showSources: boolean;
    showTimestamp: boolean;
    showActions: boolean;
    maxHeight?: number;
    expandable: boolean;
  };
  
  // Actions
  actions?: WidgetAction[];
}

interface WidgetAction {
  label: string;
  icon: string;
  action: 'navigate' | 'chat' | 'custom';
  payload?: Record<string, any>;
}
```

---

## Proactive Notifications

### Notification Types

```typescript
interface ProactiveNotification {
  id: string;
  type: 'insight' | 'alert' | 'suggestion' | 'reminder';
  
  // Content
  title: string;
  body: string;
  icon: string;
  
  // Priority
  priority: 'low' | 'normal' | 'high' | 'urgent';
  
  // Related data
  relatedShards: string[];
  insight?: InsightResponse;
  
  // Actions
  actions: NotificationAction[];
  
  // Display
  display: {
    toast: boolean;
    badge: boolean;
    sound: boolean;
    persist: boolean;
  };
  
  // Metadata
  triggeredBy: string;            // Agent ID
  triggeredAt: Date;
  expiresAt?: Date;
  
  // State
  isRead: boolean;
  isDismissed: boolean;
  actionTaken?: string;
}
```

### Rating Component

```typescript
interface FeedbackComponentProps {
  messageId: string;
  
  // Type of feedback
  type: 'thumbs' | 'rating' | 'detailed';
  
  // For detailed feedback
  categories?: FeedbackCategory[];
  allowComments?: boolean;
  
  // Callbacks
  onFeedbackSubmit: (feedback: MessageFeedback) => void;
  
  // State
  existingFeedback?: MessageFeedback;
}

type FeedbackCategory = 
  | 'inaccurate'
  | 'incomplete'
  | 'too_long'
  | 'too_short'
  | 'not_relevant'
  | 'wrong_tone'
  | 'outdated'
  | 'other';
```

---

## Prompt Management UI

> **Access**: Super Admin Only

### Overview

The Prompt Management UI enables super administrators to create, test, version, and optimize AI prompts used throughout the AI Insights system. This interface provides a sophisticated editor with live testing capabilities, version control, and A/B testing features.

---

### Prompt Management Page

**Route**: `/admin/ai-insights/prompts`

**Layout**:

**Features**:
- **Filters**: Filter by insight type, status, category
- **Table View**: List all prompts with key metadata
- **Status Indicators**: Visual badges for active/testing/deprecated
- **Performance Metrics**: Aggregated success rates, costs, response times
- **Actions**: Edit (create new version), Test, Activate/Deactivate

---

â””â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”˜
```

**Features**:
- **Monaco Editor**: Full-featured code editor with Handlebars syntax highlighting
- **Variable Management**: Define required/optional variables with validation rules
- **Model Requirements**: Specify preferred models and capabilities
- **Validation**: Real-time template syntax validation
- **Versioning**: Creating new version when updating existing prompt
- **Change Log**: Document what changed in this version

**Technical Details**:

```typescript
interface PromptEditorProps {
  prompt: PromptTemplate | null;  // null for new prompt
  onClose: () => void;
}

// Monaco Editor Configuration
const editorOptions = {
  language: 'handlebars',
  theme: 'vs-dark',
  minimap: { enabled: false },
  fontSize: 14,
  wordWrap: 'on',
  lineNumbers: 'on',
  automaticLayout: true
};

// Variable Editor
interface VariableFormFields {
  name: string;
  type: 'string' | 'number' | 'boolean' | 'array' | 'object';
  required: boolean;
  description: string;
  defaultValue?: any;
  validationRules?: {
    minLength?: number;
    maxLength?: number;
    pattern?: string;  // Regex
    enum?: any[];
  };
}
```

---

### Prompt Tester Modal

**Component**: `PromptTester`

â”‚  [Save Test Result]  [Run Another Test]                              â”‚
â”‚                                                                       â”‚
â””â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”˜
```

**Features**:
- **Input Form**: Dynamic form based on prompt variables
- **Live Testing**: Run prompt with actual AI model
- **Generated Prompt**: Show fully rendered template
- **AI Response**: Display actual AI response
- **Metrics**: Token usage, cost, response time
- **Rating**: 5-star rating for quality
- **Notes**: Free-text observations
- **Result Saving**: Test results automatically saved to prompt record

**Technical Details**:

```typescript
interface PromptTesterProps {
  prompt: PromptTemplate;
  onClose: () => void;
}

interface TestState {
  status: 'idle' | 'testing' | 'success' | 'error';
  result?: PromptTestResult;
  error?: string;
}

// Test execution
async function runTest(inputs: Record<string, any>): Promise<PromptTestResult> {
  const response = await fetch(`/api/insights/prompts/${prompt.id}/test`, {
    method: 'POST',
    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
    body: JSON.stringify({
      tenantId: prompt.tenantId,
      testInputs: inputs
    })
  });
  
  return response.json();
}
```

**Features**:
- **Test Configuration**: Set up A/B test parameters
- **Traffic Split**: Control distribution of requests
- **Real-time Results**: See metrics update live
- **Statistical Analysis**: Automatic significance testing
- **Side-by-Side Comparison**: Compare actual responses
- **Decision Actions**: Promote winner or continue testing

---

### Permission Controls

**Access Rules**:

```typescript
interface PromptManagementPermissions {
  // Only super admins can access
  canAccess: (user: User) => user.isSuperAdmin;
  
  // All prompt management actions require super admin
  canCreate: (user: User) => user.isSuperAdmin;
  canUpdate: (user: User) => user.isSuperAdmin;
  canActivate: (user: User) => user.isSuperAdmin;
  canTest: (user: User) => user.isSuperAdmin;
  canCreateABTest: (user: User) => user.isSuperAdmin;
}

// Route guard
function PromptManagementRoute() {
  const { user } = useAuth();
  
  if (!user?.isSuperAdmin) {
    return <Redirect to="/unauthorized" />;
  }
  
  return <PromptManagementPage />;
}
```

**UI Indicators**:
- Menu item only visible to super admins
- All prompt management pages show "Super Admin" badge
- Audit logs track all prompt changes with user attribution

---

### React Query Integration

**Data Fetching**:

```typescript
// List prompts
const { data: prompts } = useQuery({
  queryKey: ['prompts', filters],
  queryFn: () => fetchPrompts(filters)
});

// Get specific prompt
const { data: prompt } = useQuery({
  queryKey: ['prompt', id, tenantId],
  queryFn: () => fetchPrompt(id, tenantId)
});

// Mutations
const createMutation = useMutation({
  mutationFn: createPrompt,
  onSuccess: () => {
    queryClient.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: ['prompts'] });
  }
});

const activateMutation = useMutation({
  mutationFn: ({ id, tenantId }) => activatePrompt(id, tenantId),
  onSuccess: () => {
    queryClient.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: ['prompts'] });
  }
});

const testMutation = useMutation({
  mutationFn: ({ id, tenantId, inputs }) => testPrompt(id, tenantId, inputs)
});
```

---

## Intent Pattern Management UI (Super Admin)

> **Authorization**: Super Admin only

### Overview

Super Admins can manage intent classification patterns through a comprehensive UI with **LLM-assisted pattern creation** capabilities. This interface enables continuous improvement of intent recognition accuracy.

### Intent Pattern Management Page

**Route**: `/admin/ai-insights/intent-patterns`

**Layout**:

### Component Specifications

```typescript
interface IntentPatternManagementPageProps {
  // No props needed - Super Admin context
}

function IntentPatternManagementPage() {
  const [filters, setFilters] = useState({
    intentType: 'all',
    isActive: true,
    sortBy: 'accuracy'
  });
  
  const [llmPanelOpen, setLlmPanelOpen] = useState(false);
  const [llmWorkflow, setLlmWorkflow] = useState<'samples' | 'describe' | 'gaps' | 'optimize' | null>(null);
  
  const { data: patterns, isLoading } = useQuery({
    queryKey: ['intentPatterns', filters],
    queryFn: () => getIntentPatterns(filters)
  });
  
  const { data: metrics } = useQuery({
    queryKey: ['intentPatternMetrics'],
    queryFn: () => getIntentPatternMetrics()
  });
  
  return (
    <div className="intent-pattern-management">
      <Header
        title="Intent Pattern Management"
        subtitle="Manage and improve intent classification"
        actions={
          <>
            <Button 
              variant="secondary"
              onClick={() => setLlmPanelOpen(true)}
              icon={<Sparkles />}
            >
              ğŸ¤– AI Help
            </Button>
            <Button onClick={() => navigate('/admin/intent-patterns/new')}>
              + Create Pattern
            </Button>
          </>
        }
      />
      
      <LLMAssistantNotice />
      
      <MetricsOverview metrics={metrics} />
      
      <FilterBar filters={filters} onChange={setFilters} />
      
      <PatternList 
        patterns={patterns}
        onEdit={(id) => navigate(`/admin/intent-patterns/${id}/edit`)}
        onTest={(id) => navigate(`/admin/intent-patterns/${id}/test`)}
        onOptimize={(id) => {
          setLlmWorkflow('optimize');
          setLlmPanelOpen(true);
        }}
      />
      
      {llmPanelOpen && (
        <LLMAssistantPanel
          workflow={llmWorkflow}
          onClose={() => setLlmPanelOpen(false)}
          onWorkflowSelect={setLlmWorkflow}
        />
      )}
    </div>
  );
}

// LLM Assistant Panel Component
interface LLMAssistantPanelProps {
  workflow: 'samples' | 'describe' | 'gaps' | 'optimize' | null;
  onClose: () => void;
  onWorkflowSelect: (workflow: string) => void;
}

function LLMAssistantPanel({ workflow, onClose, onWorkflowSelect }: LLMAssistantPanelProps) {
  if (!workflow) {
    return (
      <Panel title="LLM Assistant" onClose={onClose}>
        <WorkflowSelector onSelect={onWorkflowSelect} />
      </Panel>
    );
  }
  
  switch (workflow) {
    case 'samples':
      return <GenerateFromSamplesWorkflow onClose={onClose} />;
    case 'describe':
      return <DescribeIntentWorkflow onClose={onClose} />;
    case 'gaps':
      return <AnalyzeGapsWorkflow onClose={onClose} />;
    case 'optimize':
      return <OptimizePatternWorkflow onClose={onClose} />;
  }
}

// Generate from Samples Workflow
function GenerateFromSamplesWorkflow({ onClose }: { onClose: () => void }) {
  const [samples, setSamples] = useState<string[]>(['', '', '', '', '']);
  const [targetIntent, setTargetIntent] = useState('');
  const [targetSubtype, setTargetSubtype] = useState('');
  
  const generateMutation = useMutation({
    mutationFn: () => suggestPatternsFromSamples({
      samples: samples.filter(s => s.trim()),
      targetIntent,
      targetSubtype
    })
  });
  
  return (
    <Panel title="Generate from Samples" onClose={onClose}>
      <FormField label="Target Intent">
        <Select value={targetIntent} onChange={setTargetIntent}>
          <option value="analysis">Analysis</option>
          <option value="summary">Summary</option>
          <option value="comparison">Comparison</option>
          {/* ... */}
        </Select>
      </FormField>
      
      <FormField label="Subtype (Optional)">
        <Select value={targetSubtype} onChange={setTargetSubtype}>
          <option value="">Any</option>
          <option value="risk">Risk</option>
          <option value="opportunity">Opportunity</option>
          {/* ... */}
        </Select>
      </FormField>
      
      <FormField label="Sample Queries (5-10)">
        {samples.map((sample, i) => (
          <Input
            key={i}
            value={sample}
            onChange={(e) => {
              const newSamples = [...samples];
              newSamples[i] = e.target.value;
              setSamples(newSamples);
            }}
            placeholder={`Sample ${i + 1}`}
          />
        ))}
        <Button variant="text" onClick={() => setSamples([...samples, ''])}>
          + Add More
        </Button>
      </FormField>
      
      <Button
        onClick={() => generateMutation.mutate()}
        disabled={samples.filter(s => s.trim()).length < 3}
        loading={generateMutation.isPending}
      >
        Analyze Samples
      </Button>
      
      {generateMutation.data && (
        <SuggestedPatternsResult 
          suggestions={generateMutation.data}
          onCreatePattern={(pattern) => {
            // Create pattern and close
          }}
        />
      )}
    </Panel>
  );
}
```

## Web Search Configuration UI

> **Authorization**: Super Admin (provider management) and Tenant Admin (per-tenant settings)
> **Related Documentation**: [Web Search Integration](./WEB-SEARCH.md), [Web Search API](./API.md#web-search-api)

### Super Admin: Web Search Provider Management

Super admins manage global web search providers, their configurations, and provider health.

---

## Recurring Search Management

> **Authorization**: Authenticated User (sees own + shared searches), Tenant Admin (sees all)

### Overview

The Recurring Search Management page allows users to create, configure, and monitor recurring searches with AI-powered alert detection. Users can set up searches that run automatically on a schedule and receive alerts when significant changes are detected.

---

### Recurring Searches List Page

**Route**: `/insights/recurring-searches`

#### Features

**Search List Table**:
- **Columns**:
  - Name with emoji icon based on search type
  - Type (Sales Opportunity, Risk Monitoring, Competitor, Regulatory, Custom)
  - Schedule (frequency + time)
  - Last execution time (relative)
  - Alert count with visual indicator (â—â—â—â—â— = high alerts)
  - Status badge (âœ… Active, â¸ï¸ Paused)
- **Row Actions**:
  - Pause/Resume toggle
  - Edit search configuration
  - Duplicate (create copy)
  - View execution history
  - More menu (Delete, Share with team, Test run)
- **Filters**:
  - Search type dropdown
  - Status filter (All, Active, Paused)
  - Text search by name
  - Sort by: Name, Next Execution, Alert Count, Created Date

**Empty State**:
```

```

#### Form Validation

| Field | Validation |
|-------|------------|
| Name | Required, 3-100 characters |
| Query | Required, 10-500 characters |
| Type | Required selection |
| Data Sources | At least one source selected |
| Schedule | Valid time in tenant timezone |
| Confidence Threshold | 0.5-1.0 (50%-100%) |

#### Test Run Feature

When user clicks "Test Run":
1. Execute search immediately with current configuration
2. Show preview modal with results
3. Display confidence scores for any detected alerts
4. Allow user to adjust configuration before saving

---

**Route**: `/insights/recurring-searches/{id}/results`

---

## Alert Dashboard

> **Authorization**: Authenticated User (own alerts), Tenant Admin (all tenant alerts)

### Overview

The Alert Dashboard is the central hub for viewing, managing, and providing feedback on alerts generated by recurring searches. It prioritizes unread and high-confidence alerts.

---

### Alert Feed Page

**Route**: `/insights/alerts`

#### Layout

```

#### Alert Card Features

**Confidence Badge**:
- âš ï¸ HIGH (80-100%): Red/orange badge
- â„¹ï¸ MEDIUM (60-79%): Blue badge
- ğŸ’¡ LOW (50-59%): Gray badge

**Quick Actions**:
- **âœ… Relevant**: Mark as relevant (trains learning system)
- **âŒ Not Relevant**: Mark as false positive (creates suppression rule option)
- **ğŸ’¤ Snooze**: Temporarily hide (1 hour, 1 day, 1 week, custom)
- **View Details**: Open detailed alert view

**Visual Indicators**:
- Unread alerts: Bold text + blue left border
- Snoozed alerts: Grayed out with snooze icon
- Read alerts: Normal text

---

## Recurring Search Statistics

> **Authorization**: Tenant Admin (own tenant), Super Admin (all tenants)

### Overview

Statistics dashboards provide insights into recurring search performance, alert accuracy, and learning system effectiveness. Tenant Admins see tenant-level data, Super Admins see global data.

---

### Tenant Statistics Dashboard

**Route**: `/admin/recurring-searches/statistics`

```

#### Features

**Time Period Selector**:
- Last 7 days
- Last 30 days
- Last 90 days
- Last 1 year
- Custom range

**Metrics Cards**:
- Active Searches (with trend)
- Total Alerts (with recent change)
- Alert Accuracy % (with trend indicator)
- Quota Usage (with visual gauge)

**Charts**:
- Alert Accuracy Trend (line chart over time)
- False Positive Rate Trend
- Alerts by Search Type (bar chart)
- Execution Success Rate

**Tables**:
- Performance by search type
- Top performing searches (by accuracy)
- Most active searches (by alert count)
- Quota usage by user

**Export Options**:
- CSV export
- PDF report
- Excel workbook

---

## Recurring Search Configuration

> **Authorization**: Tenant Admin (own tenant), Super Admin (all tenants)

### Overview

Configuration interface for tenant-wide recurring search settings, including default thresholds, digest mode, data retention, and learning system toggles.

---

### Tenant Configuration Page

**Route**: `/admin/recurring-searches/configuration`

#### Layout

```

---

## Tenant Admin Configuration UI

> **Authorization**: Tenant Admin only (or Super Admin)
```

### Overview

Tenant admins need a simplified configuration interface to customize AI behavior for their organization without modifying system-level settings. This interface allows:

- **Model Selection**: Choose default models and fallbacks
- **Budget Management**: Set spending limits and alerts
- **Custom Prompts**: Create tenant-specific prompt variations (inheriting from system prompts)
- **Feature Control**: Enable/disable AI features for the tenant
- **Privacy Settings**: Configure data retention and handling policies

---

### Tenant AI Configuration Page

**Route**: `/admin/ai-configuration`

**Layout**:

### Component Specifications

```typescript
interface TenantAIConfigurationPageProps {
  tenantId: string;
}

function TenantAIConfigurationPage({ tenantId }: TenantAIConfigurationPageProps) {
  const [activeTab, setActiveTab] = useState<'general' | 'models' | 'prompts' | 'budget' | 'privacy'>('general');
  
  const { data: config, isLoading } = useQuery({
    queryKey: ['tenantAIConfig', tenantId],
    queryFn: () => getTenantAIConfig(tenantId)
  });
  
  const updateMutation = useMutation({
    mutationFn: (updates: Partial<TenantAIConfiguration>) => 
      updateTenantAIConfig(tenantId, updates),
    onSuccess: () => {
      toast.success('Configuration updated successfully');
      queryClient.invalidateQueries(['tenantAIConfig', tenantId]);
    }
  });
  
  return (
    <div className="tenant-ai-configuration">
      <Header
        title="AI Configuration"
        subtitle="Customize AI behavior for your organization"
        actions={
          <Button 
            onClick={() => updateMutation.mutate(config)}
            disabled={!config || updateMutation.isPending}
          >
            ğŸ’¾ Save
          </Button>
        }
      />
      
      <Tabs value={activeTab} onChange={setActiveTab}>
        <Tab value="general">General</Tab>
        <Tab value="models">Models</Tab>
        <Tab value="prompts">Prompts</Tab>
        <Tab value="budget">Budget</Tab>
        <Tab value="privacy">Privacy</Tab>
      </Tabs>
      
      <TabContent>
        {activeTab === 'general' && <GeneralTab config={config} onChange={updateMutation.mutate} />}
        {activeTab === 'models' && <ModelsTab config={config} onChange={updateMutation.mutate} />}
        {activeTab === 'prompts' && <TenantPromptsTab tenantId={tenantId} />}
        {activeTab === 'budget' && <BudgetTab config={config} tenantId={tenantId} onChange={updateMutation.mutate} />}
        {activeTab === 'privacy' && <PrivacyTab config={config} onChange={updateMutation.mutate} />}
      </TabContent>
    </div>
  );
}

// General Tab
interface GeneralTabProps {
  config: TenantAIConfiguration;
  onChange: (updates: Partial<TenantAIConfiguration>) => void;
}

function GeneralTab({ config, onChange }: GeneralTabProps) {
  return (
    <div className="general-tab">
      <Section title="Features">
        <CheckboxGroup
          value={config.features}
          onChange={(features) => onChange({ features })}
          options={[
            {
              value: 'enableProactiveInsights',
              label: 'Proactive Insights',
              description: 'AI suggests insights without being asked'
            },
            {
              value: 'enableToolCalling',
              label: 'Tool Calling',
              description: 'AI can perform actions (create tasks, send emails)'
            },
            {
              value: 'enableMultiModal',
              label: 'Multi-Modal Analysis',
              description: 'Process images and documents (beta)',
              badge: 'Beta'
            },
            {
              value: 'enableSemanticCache',
              label: 'Semantic Cache',
              description: 'Faster responses for similar queries'
            },
            {
              value: 'enableConversationMemory',
              label: 'Conversation Memory',
              description: 'Remember context across conversations'
            }
          ]}
        />
      </Section>
      
      <Section title="Branding">
        <FormField label="Assistant Name">
          <Input
            value={config.branding?.assistantName}
            onChange={(e) => onChange({
              branding: { ...config.branding, assistantName: e.target.value }
            })}
            placeholder="e.g., Acme AI Assistant"
          />
        </FormField>
        
        <FormField label="Avatar URL">
          <Input
            value={config.branding?.assistantAvatar}
            onChange={(e) => onChange({
              branding: { ...config.branding, assistantAvatar: e.target.value }
            })}
            placeholder="https://cdn.example.com/avatar.png"
          />
          <AvatarPreview
            name={config.branding?.assistantName}
            avatar={config.branding?.assistantAvatar}
          />
        </FormField>
        
        <FormField label="Welcome Message">
          <TextArea
            value={config.branding?.welcomeMessage}
            onChange={(e) => onChange({
              branding: { ...config.branding, welcomeMessage: e.target.value }
            })}
            rows={3}
            placeholder="Hello! How can I help you today?"
          />
        </FormField>
        
        <FormField label="Primary Color">
          <ColorPicker
            value={config.branding?.primaryColor}
            onChange={(color) => onChange({
              branding: { ...config.branding, primaryColor: color }
            })}
          />
        </FormField>
      </Section>
    </div>
  );
}

// Budget Tab
interface BudgetTabProps {
  config: TenantAIConfiguration;
  tenantId: string;
  onChange: (updates: Partial<TenantAIConfiguration>) => void;
}

function BudgetTab({ config, tenantId, onChange }: BudgetTabProps) {
  const { data: budgetStatus } = useQuery({
    queryKey: ['budgetStatus', tenantId],
    queryFn: () => getBudgetStatus(tenantId),
    refetchInterval: 30000 // Refresh every 30s
  });
  
  const { data: usage } = useQuery({
    queryKey: ['tenantUsage', tenantId],
    queryFn: () => getTenantUsage(tenantId, {
      startDate: startOfMonth(new Date()),
      endDate: new Date()
    })
  });
  
  return (
    <div className="budget-tab">
      <Section title="Current Usage">
        <BudgetProgressCard
          current={budgetStatus?.currentSpend || 0}
          limit={config.budget?.monthlyLimitUSD || 0}
          projected={budgetStatus?.projectedEndOfMonth}
          insights={budgetStatus?.insights}
        />
      </Section>
      
      <Section title="Budget Limits">
        <FormField label="Monthly Limit (USD)">
          <Input
            type="number"
            value={config.budget?.monthlyLimitUSD}
            onChange={(e) => onChange({
              budget: { ...config.budget, monthlyLimitUSD: Number(e.target.value) }
            })}
          />
        </FormField>
        
        <FormField label="Daily Limit (USD)">
          <Input
            type="number"
            value={config.budget?.dailyLimitUSD}
            onChange={(e) => onChange({
              budget: { ...config.budget, dailyLimitUSD: Number(e.target.value) }
            })}
          />
        </FormField>
        
        <FormField label="Max Cost Per Insight (USD)">
          <Input
            type="number"
            step="0.01"
            value={config.budget?.costPerInsight?.max}
            onChange={(e) => onChange({
              budget: {
                ...config.budget,
                costPerInsight: { ...config.budget?.costPerInsight, max: Number(e.target.value) }
              }
            })}
          />
        </FormField>
      </Section>
      
      <Section title="Alerts">
        <AlertThresholdList
          thresholds={config.budget?.alertThresholds || []}
          onChange={(thresholds) => onChange({
            budget: { ...config.budget, alertThresholds: thresholds }
          })}
        />
      </Section>
      
      <Section title="Usage Breakdown">
        {usage && (
          <>
            <UsageChart
              data={usage.byModel}
              type="model"
              title="By Model"
            />
            <UsageChart
              data={usage.byInsightType}
              type="insightType"
              title="By Insight Type"
            />
            <Button onClick={() => downloadUsageReport(tenantId)}>
              ğŸ“¥ Download Report
            </Button>
          </>
        )}
      </Section>
    </div>
  );
}

// Tenant Prompts Tab
interface TenantPromptsTabProps {
  tenantId: string;
}

function TenantPromptsTab({ tenantId }: TenantPromptsTabProps) {
  const navigate = useNavigate();
  
  const { data, isLoading } = useQuery({
    queryKey: ['tenantPrompts', tenantId],
    queryFn: () => getTenantPrompts(tenantId)
  });
  
  const activateMutation = useMutation({
    mutationFn: ({ id }: { id: string }) => activateTenantPrompt(id, tenantId),
    onSuccess: () => {
      toast.success('Prompt activated successfully');
      queryClient.invalidateQueries(['tenantPrompts', tenantId]);
    }
  });
  
  const deactivateMutation = useMutation({
    mutationFn: ({ id }: { id: string }) => deactivateTenantPrompt(id, tenantId),
    onSuccess: () => {
      toast.success('Prompt deactivated successfully');
      queryClient.invalidateQueries(['tenantPrompts', tenantId]);
    }
  });
  
  return (
    <div className="tenant-prompts-tab">
      <div className="header">
        <div>
          <h3>Custom Prompts</h3>
          <p>Create custom prompts that inherit from system prompts and add tenant-specific instructions.</p>
        </div>
        <Button onClick={() => navigate(`/admin/ai-configuration/prompts/new`)}>
          + New Prompt
        </Button>
      </div>
      
      {data?.tenantPrompts.map((prompt) => (
        <TenantPromptCard
          key={prompt.id}
          prompt={prompt}
          onEdit={() => navigate(`/admin/ai-configuration/prompts/${prompt.id}/edit`)}
          onActivate={() => activateMutation.mutate({ id: prompt.id })}
          onDeactivate={() => deactivateMutation.mutate({ id: prompt.id })}
        />
      ))}
      
      {data?.tenantPrompts.length === 0 && (
        <EmptyState
          icon="ğŸ“"
          title="No custom prompts yet"
          description="Create your first custom prompt to tailor AI responses for your organization."
          action={
            <Button onClick={() => navigate(`/admin/ai-configuration/prompts/new`)}>
              Create Prompt
            </Button>
          }
        />
      )}
    </div>
  );
}
```

---

## Component Library

### Core Components

```typescript
// AI Avatar
interface AIAvatarProps {
  size: 'sm' | 'md' | 'lg';
  isThinking?: boolean;
  customIcon?: string;
}

// Confidence Badge
interface ConfidenceBadgeProps {
  level: 'high' | 'medium' | 'low';
  score?: number;
  showScore?: boolean;
}

// Citation Link
interface CitationLinkProps {
  citation: SourceCitation;
  index: number;
  onClick?: () => void;
  showPreview?: boolean;
}

// Insight Card
interface InsightCardProps {
  insight: InsightResponse;
  compact?: boolean;
  showActions?: boolean;
  showSources?: boolean;
  onAction?: (action: InsightAction) => void;
}

// Suggestion Chip
interface SuggestionChipProps {
  label: string;
  icon?: string;
  onClick: () => void;
}

// Streaming Text
interface StreamingTextProps {
  content: string;
  isStreaming: boolean;
  cursorStyle?: 'bar' | 'block' | 'none';
}

// Source Preview
interface SourcePreviewProps {
  citation: SourceCitation;
  onNavigate?: () => void;
}

// Action Button
interface ActionButtonProps {
  action: InsightAction;
  variant: 'primary' | 'secondary' | 'ghost';
  size: 'sm' | 'md';
  onClick: () => void;
}
```

### Composition Examples

```tsx
// Chat Message Component
function ChatMessage({ message }: { message: ChatMessage }) {
  return (
    <div className={`chat-message ${message.role}`}>
      <div className="message-header">
        {message.role === 'assistant' ? (
          <AIAvatar size="sm" isThinking={message.metadata?.isStreaming} />
        ) : (
          <UserAvatar user={currentUser} size="sm" />
        )}
        <span className="sender-name">
          {message.role === 'assistant' ? 'Castiel' : 'You'}
        </span>
        <span className="timestamp">
          {formatTime(message.timestamp)}
        </span>
      </div>
      
      <div className="message-content">
        {message.metadata?.isStreaming ? (
          <StreamingText 
            content={message.content} 
            isStreaming={true}
          />
        ) : (
          <Markdown content={message.content} />
        )}
        
        {message.metadata?.citations && (
          <div className="citations">
            {message.metadata.citations.map((citation, i) => (
              <CitationLink 
                key={citation.id}
                citation={citation}
                index={i + 1}
                showPreview
              />
            ))}
          </div>
        )}
        
        {message.metadata?.confidence && (
          <ConfidenceBadge 
            level={message.metadata.confidence.level}
            score={message.metadata.confidence.score}
          />
        )}
      </div>
      
      {message.role === 'assistant' && !message.metadata?.isStreaming && (
        <div className="message-actions">
          <FeedbackButtons messageId={message.id} />
          <ActionButtons actions={message.metadata?.actions || []} />
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}
```

## Responsive Design

### Breakpoints

```typescript
const BREAKPOINTS = {
  mobile: 640,
  tablet: 768,
  desktop: 1024,
  wide: 1280,
};

interface ResponsiveConfig {
  mobile: {
    chatMode: 'fullscreen';
    quickPanelPosition: 'bottom';
    widgetColumns: 1;
  };
  tablet: {
    chatMode: 'panel';
    quickPanelPosition: 'right';
    widgetColumns: 2;
  };
  desktop: {
    chatMode: 'panel';
    quickPanelPosition: 'right';
    widgetColumns: 3;
  };
}
```

## Accessibility

### Requirements

```typescript
interface AccessibilityRequirements {
  // Screen reader support
  ariaLabels: {
    chatInput: 'Ask AI assistant';
    sendButton: 'Send message';
    feedbackPositive: 'Mark as helpful';
    feedbackNegative: 'Mark as not helpful';
    closePanel: 'Close AI panel';
  };
  
  // Keyboard navigation
  keyboardNav: {
    focusTrap: true;              // Keep focus in chat panel
    escapeToClose: true;
    arrowNavigation: true;        // Navigate messages
  };
  
  // Visual
  visual: {
    minContrastRatio: 4.5;
    focusIndicators: true;
    reducedMotion: true;          // Respect prefers-reduced-motion
  };
  
  // Content
  content: {
    altTextForCharts: true;
    captionsForAudio: true;
    structuredHeadings: true;
  };
}
```
